# A04.2.00.001
- ## Term
	- EN: "Muscles of neck"
	- LA: "Musculi colli"
	- ES: "Músculos del cuello"

# A04.2.01.001
- ## Term
	- EN: "Platysma"
	- LA: "Platysma"
	- ES: "Platisma"
- ## Data
	- ### Anatomy
		- Configuration
			- Broad muscle
		- Conformation
			- Origin
				- Scapular girdle
				- Fascia covering deltoid
				- Fascia covering pectorals major
			- Insertion
				- Mental skin
				- Inferior border of mandible
				- Lower face skin
		- Action
			- Tense skin of neck
			- Draw corners of mouth inferiorly
		- Arteries
			- Submental artery
			- Supraescapular artery
		- Nerves
			- Cervical branch of facial nerve

# A04.2.01.002
- ## Term
	- EN: "Longus colli"
	- LA: "M. longus colli"
	- ES: "Músculo largo del cuello"
- ## Data
	- ### Anatomy
		- Constitution
			- Striated muscle tissue
		- Configuration
			- Long triangular muscle
		- Conformation
			- Longitudinal portion
				- Origin
					- Anterior of tubercle C4-C6 vertebrae
					- Body of T1-T3 vertebrae
				- Insertion
					- Body of C2-C4 vertebrae
			- Superolateral portion
				- Origin
					- Transverse process of C3-C5
				- Insertion
					- Anterior tubercle of atlas
			- Inferolateral portion
				- Origin
					- Body of T1-T3 vertebrae
				- Insertion
					- Transverse process of C5-C7 vertebrae
		- Arteries
			- Ascending cervical artery
			- Inferior thyroid artery
		- Nerves
			- Anterior rami of C2-C6 spinal nerves
		- Action
			- Flexion of neck
			- Ipsilateral rotation of neck

# A04.2.01.003
- ## Term
	- EN: "Longus capitis"
	- LA: "M. longus capitis"
	- ES: "Músculo largo de la cabeza"

			- Inferior thyroid artery
		- Nerves
			- Anterior rami of C1-C3 spinal nerves
		- Action
			- Flexion of head

# A04.2.01.008
- ## Term
	- EN: "Sternocleidomastoid"
	- LA: "M. sternocleidomastoideus"
	- ES: "Músculo esternocleidomastoideo"
- ## Data
	- ### Anatomy
		- Configuration
			- Long muscle
		- Conformation
			- Sternal head
				- Origin
					- Manubrium of sternum
				- Insertion
					- Mastoid process
					- Superior nuchal line
			- Cleido-occipital head
				- Origin
					- Medial third of clavicle
				- Insertion
					- Superior nuchal line
			- Cleido-mastoid head
				- Origin
					- Medial third of clavicle
				- Insertion
					- Mastoid process
		- Arteries
			- Occipital artery
			- Superior thyroid artery
		- Nerves
			- Motor
				- Accessory nerve
			- Sensory
				- Cervical plexus
		- Action
			- Ipsilateral Lateral flexion of head
			- Ipsilateral rotation of head
			- Flexion of head
			- Elevate sternum and clavicles

		- Conformation

				- Lateral mass of atlas
			- Insertion

				- Petrous part of temporal bone

				- Ipsilateral Lateral flexion of head
		- Arteries

			- Inferior thyroid artery
		- Nerves

# A04.2.02.003

        - Conformation

# A04.2.03.002
- ## Term
	- EN: "Digastric"
	- LA: "M. digastricus"
	- ES: "Músculo digástrico"
- ## Data
	- Anatomy
		- Constitution
			- Striated muscle tissue
		- Configuration
			- Long muscle
		- Conformation
			- Anterior belly
				- Origin
					- Digastric fossa of mandible
				- Insertion
					- Intermediate tendon
			- Posterior belly
				- Origin
					- Mastoid notch of temporal bone
				- Insertion
					- Intermediate tendon
		- Arteries
			- Occipital artery
			- Submental branch of the facial artery
		- Nerves
			- Digastric (preparotid) branch of facial nerve (CN VII)
		- Action
			- Elevation of hyoid bone
			- Depression of mandible

				- Articular processes of vertebrae C4-C7
				- Transverse processes of vertebrae T1-T6
			- Insertion
				- Between superior and inferior nuchal lines of occipital bone
		- Arteries
			- Descending branch of occipital artery
			- Deep cervical artery
		- Nerves
			- Descending branches of greater occipital nerve (C2)
			- Spinal nerve C3
		- Action
			- Extension of head
			- Lateral flexion of head

# A06.2.01.001
- ## Term
	- EN: "Larynx"
	- LA: "Larynx"
	- ES: "Laringe"
- ## Data
	- Anatomy
		- Constitution
			- Pharynx
		- Configuration
			- Shape
				- Cylinder
			- External
				- Anterior facet
				- Posterior facet
			- Internal
		- Conformation
			- Skeleton
				- Cricoid cartilage
				- Thyroid cartilage
				- Epiglottic cartilage
				- Arytenoid cartilage
				- Corniculate cartilage
				- Cuneiform cartilage
			- Joints
				- Intrinsic
					- Cricothyroid joint
					- Median cricothyroid ligament
					- Crico-arytenoid joint
					- Cricopharyngeal ligament
					- Thyro-epiglottic ligament
					- Vocal ligament
					- Vestibular ligament
					- Quadrangular membrane
				- Extrinsic
					- Thyrohyoid membrane
					- Hyo-epiglottic ligament
					- Cricotracheal ligament
			- Muscles
				- Intrinsc
					- Cricothyroid muscle
					- Posterior crico-arytenoid
					- Lateral crico-arytenoid
					- Vocalis
					- Thyro-arytenoid
					- Oblique arytenoid
					- Transverse arytenoid
				- Extrinsic
					- Sternothyroid muscle
					- Thyrohyoid muscle
					- Stylopharyngeus
					- Palatopharyngeus
					- Inferior pharyngeal constrictor
		- Ateries
			- Superior laryngeal artery
			- Inferior laryngeal artery
			- Cricothyroid branch
		- Veins
			- Superior laryngeal vein
			- Inferior laryngeal vein
		- Nerves
			- Superior laryngeal nerve
			- Recurrent laryngeal nerve
